This present F R I D A Y ,
Will be prefented a N E W

PLAN

A U G U S T 17, 1781,
of E N T E R T A I N M E N T ,

call'd

The School of Shakefpeare;
H U M O U R S and P A S S I O N S .
Given in a Regular Reprefentation of several oS his most Favourite and Capital
1
Scenes in H A M L E T , the Second Part of HENRY IV. HENRY VIII.
and ROMEO and JULIET.
With DreJJ'es and Scenery, fuited to the Characters and their Situations.
The inimitable Scenes of the Poet, selected sor the Purpose, and digested into
Four Acts, will exemplify, in the strongest Colours of our immortal Bard,

FILIAL P I E T Y , P A R E N T A L T E N D E R N E S S , AMB I T I O N , and LOVE.
